Growers must be accredited to the world\u2019s leading ethical wool standard, ZQ, to qualify for the ZQRX programme. ZQRX wool is underpinned by a powerful technology engine (RX). Unlike other regenerative tools that simply report historical data, RX uses real-time metrics, machine learning, and user-friendly modelling to help growers and brands accurately plan, predict and improve their ESG outcomes.
